• In 2021 the U.S. District Court for the Western District of Michigan dismissed Baier v. Biden (1:21-cv-00843) which attempted to challenge the 2020 election results; the court sanctioned the plaintiffs for filing a frivolous suit.  
• In 2022 the U.S. District Court for the District of Columbia dismissed Palin v. Biden (1:22-cv-01415), a defamation suit against Biden over social-media posts; the court granted Biden’s motion to dismiss under D.C.’s anti-SLAPP statute.
